@prefix : <http://mapping.example.com/> .
@prefix edifact-o: <https://purl.org/edifact/ontology#> .
@prefix rdf: <http://www.w3.org/1999/02/22-rdf-syntax-ns#> .
@prefix sh: <http://www.w3.org/ns/shacl#> .
@prefix xsd: <http://www.w3.org/2001/XMLSchema#> .

:Dokumentenname a sh:NodeShape ;
    sh:property [ sh:datatype xsd:string ;
            sh:in ( "Commercial invoice" "Credit advice" "Value credit" "Value debit" "Handelsrechnung" "Gutschriftsanzeige" "Wertgutschrift" "Wertbelastung" ) ;
            sh:maxCount 1 ;
            sh:message "Data element 1001 is missing in the BGM segment" ;
            sh:minCount 1 ;
            sh:path edifact-o:hasDocumentType ] ;
    sh:targetClass edifact-o:InvoiceDetails .


The SHACL shape :Dokumentenname targets all instances of the class edifact-o:InvoiceDetails, enforcing a constraint on the property edifact-o:hasDocumentType, which must have exactly one string value (xsd:string) that is one of the following: "Commercial invoice", "Credit advice", "Value credit", "Value debit", "Handelsrechnung", "Gutschriftsanzeige", "Wertgutschrift", or "Wertbelastung", with a validation failure message "Data element 1001 is missing in the BGM segment" if this property is missing or its value is outside this list.

@prefix sh: <http://www.w3.org/ns/shacl#> .
@prefix xsd: <http://www.w3.org/2001/XMLSchema#> .

:UmsatzsteuernummerKaeufer a sh:NodeShape ;
    sh:message "The Segemnt RFF+VA is missing for the Segemnet NAD+BY, i.e. the buyer's VAT number is missing" ;
    sh:or ( [ sh:not [ a sh:PropertyShape ;
                        sh:hasValue "http://example.com/BuyerRole" ;
                        sh:path rdf:type ] ] [ sh:maxCount 1 ;
                sh:maxLength 14 ;
                sh:minCount 1 ;
                sh:path p2p-o-org:VATIdentifier ] ) ;
    sh:targetClass org:FormalOrganization .


The SHACL shape :UmsatzsteuernummerKaeufer applies to all instances of the class org:FormalOrganization, requiring that if they have the RDF type "http://example.com/BuyerRole", then they must have exactly one p2p-o-org:VATIdentifier property with a string value of maximum 14 characters; otherwise, validation will fail with the message "The Segment RFF+VA is missing for the Segment NAD+BY, i.e. the buyer's VAT number is missing".

Translation #88
@prefix : <http://mapping.example.com/> .
@prefix edifact-o: <https://purl.org/edifact/ontology#> .
@prefix sh: <http://www.w3.org/ns/shacl#> .
@prefix xsd: <http://www.w3.org/2001/XMLSchema#> .

:SumNetPrice a sh:NodeShape ;
    sh:sparql [ a sh:SPARQLConstraint ;
            sh:message "edifact-o:hasTotalLineItemAmount must equal the sum of all values of edifact-o:hasLineItemAmount" ;
            sh:prefixes [ sh:declare [ sh:namespace "https://purl.org/edifact/ontology#"^^xsd:anyURI ;
                            sh:prefix "edifact-o" ] ] ;
            sh:select """SELECT $this (edifact-o:hasTotalLineItemAmount AS ?path) (?totalAmount AS ?value)
            WHERE { 
                $this a edifact-o:InvoiceDetails ;
                    edifact-o:hasTotalLineItemAmount ?totalAmount .
                    {select $this (sum(?itemAmount) as ?sum) {
                        ?item edifact-o:isItemOf ?invoice ; edifact-o:hasLineItemAmount ?itemAmount.
                        ?invoice edifact-o:hasInvoiceDetails $this.
                        } 
                        group by $this }
                FILTER (?sum != ?totalAmount) 
                }""" ] ;
    sh:targetClass edifact-o:InvoiceDetails .


The SHACL shape :SumNetPrice targets all instances of the class edifact-o:InvoiceDetails, requiring each instance to have exactly one edifact-o:hasTotalLineItemAmount property value that equals the sum of all edifact-o:hasLineItemAmount property values associated with its line items; if this constraint is violated, validation will fail with the message "edifact-o:hasTotalLineItemAmount must equal the sum of all values of edifact-o:hasLineItemAmount".
----

@prefix sh: <http://www.w3.org/ns/shacl#> .
@prefix xsd: <http://www.w3.org/2001/XMLSchema#> .

:InvoiceConditionalDiscountShape a sh:NodeShape ;
    sh:message "If no discount is applied, discount amount must be greater than 0." ;
    sh:or ( [ sh:property [ sh:hasValue true ;
                        sh:path p2p-o-item:discountApplied ] ] [ sh:property [ sh:datatype xsd:float ;
                        sh:minInclusive 0.01 ;
                        sh:path p2p-o-item:discountAmount ] ] ) ;
    sh:targetClass p2p-o-item:InvoiceLineItem .


The SHACL shape :InvoiceConditionalDiscountShape applies to all instances of the class p2p-o-item:InvoiceLineItem, specifying that either the property p2p-o-item:discountApplied must have the value true, or the property p2p-o-item:discountAmount must have a value that is a float greater than or equal to 0.01; if neither condition is met, the validation will fail with the message "If no discount is applied, discount amount must be greater than 0."

@prefix : <http://mapping.example.com/> .
@prefix foaf: <http://xmlns.com/foaf/0.1/> .
@prefix rdf: <http://www.w3.org/1999/02/22-rdf-syntax-ns#> .
@prefix sh: <http://www.w3.org/ns/shacl#> .
@prefix xsd: <http://www.w3.org/2001/XMLSchema#> .

:ClientProfileCompletionDependency a sh:NodeShape ;
    sh:and ( [ sh:property [ sh:hasValue true ;
                        sh:path :profileComplete ] ] [ sh:property [ sh:minLength 3 ;
                        sh:path foaf:name ] ] [ sh:property [ sh:path foaf:mbox ;
                        sh:pattern "^[\\w.-]+@[\\w.-]+\\.\\w{2,}$" ] ] ) ;
    sh:message "To mark a profile as complete, name and valid email must be present." ;
    sh:targetClass foaf:Person .


The SHACL shape :ClientProfileCompletionDependency targets all instances of the class foaf:Person, enforcing a validation rule that requires the presence and validity of three specific properties: :profileComplete with a value of true, foaf:name with a minimum length of 3 characters, and foaf:mbox with a valid email address pattern. Failure to meet these conditions will result in a validation error with the message "To mark a profile as complete, name and valid email must be present."
----

:ClientEmailOrPhoneRequired a sh:NodeShape ;
    sh:message "Client must provide at least one contact method: email or phone." ;
    sh:or ( [ sh:property [ sh:minCount 1 ;
                        sh:path foaf:mbox ] ] [ sh:property [ sh:minCount 1 ;
                        sh:path vcard:hasTelephone ] ] ) ;
    sh:targetClass foaf:Person .


The SHACL shape :ClientEmailOrPhoneRequired applies to all instances of the class foaf:Person, specifying that at least one of the following conditions must be met: the property foaf:mbox (email) must appear at least once or the property vcard:hasTelephone (phone) must appear at least once, otherwise, the validation will fail with the message "Client must provide at least one contact method: email or phone."

@prefix sh: <http://www.w3.org/ns/shacl#> .
@prefix xsd: <http://www.w3.org/2001/XMLSchema#> .

:ShippingManifestIncotermsShape a sh:NodeShape ;
    sh:message "Incoterms code must be one of: EXW, FOB, CIF, or DDP." ;
    sh:property [ sh:datatype xsd:string ;
            sh:in ( "EXW" "FOB" "CIF" "DDP" ) ;
            sh:path p2p-o:incotermsCode ] ;
    sh:targetClass p2p-o:ShippingManifest .


The SHACL shape :ShippingManifestIncotermsShape targets all instances of the class p2p-o:ShippingManifest, requiring them to have exactly one value for the property p2p-o:incotermsCode, which must be a string (xsd:string) and must be one of the following allowed values: "EXW", "FOB", "CIF", or "DDP"; if the value is missing or does not match one of these allowed values, validation will fail with the message: "Incoterms code must be one of: EXW, FOB, CIF, or DDP."

@prefix xsd: <http://www.w3.org/2001/XMLSchema#> .

:TicketAndEventSyncShape a sh:NodeShape ;
    sh:sparql [ a sh:SPARQLConstraint ;
            sh:message "Ticket purchase time must be before the event start time." ;
            sh:prefixes [ sh:declare [ sh:namespace "http://schema.org/"^^xsd:anyURI ;
                            sh:prefix "schema" ] ] ;
            sh:select """
            SELECT $this WHERE {
                $this schema:datePurchased ?purchaseTime .
                $this schema:isPartOf ?event .
                ?event schema:startDate ?startTime .
                FILTER (?purchaseTime > ?startTime)
            }
        """ ] ;
    sh:targetClass schema1:Ticket .


The SHACL shape :TicketAndEventSyncShape targets all instances of the class schema1:Ticket, enforcing a constraint that each ticket must have exactly one purchase time (schema:datePurchased) and exactly one associated event with a start time (schema:startDate and schema:isPartOf), whereby the purchase time must be before the event start time; if this temporal relationship is not respected, validation will fail with the message: "Ticket purchase time must be before the event start time."

:ReceiptSparqlTotalMatchShape a sh:NodeShape ;
    sh:sparql [ a sh:SPARQLConstraint ;
            sh:message "Total amount must match sum of all line item prices." ;
            sh:prefixes [ sh:declare [ sh:namespace "http://schema.org/"^^xsd:anyURI ;
                            sh:prefix "schema" ] ] ;
            sh:select """
            SELECT $this WHERE {
                $this schema:totalPaymentDue ?total .
                {
                    SELECT $this (SUM(?price) AS ?calculatedTotal)
                    WHERE {
                        $this schema:mainEntity ?item .
                        ?item schema:price ?price .
                    } GROUP BY $this
                }
                FILTER (?total != ?calculatedTotal)
            }
        """ ] ;
    sh:targetClass schema1:Invoice .


The SHACL shape :ReceiptSparqlTotalMatchShape targets all instances of the class schema1:Invoice, specifying that each instance must have a total payment due (schema:totalPaymentDue) equal to the sum of all line item prices (schema:mainEntity/schema:price), with a validation failure message "Total amount must match sum of all line item prices" if the two totals do not match.

:ReviewSpamFilterShape a sh:NodeShape ;
    sh:sparql [ a sh:SPARQLConstraint ;
            sh:message "Review must not contain spam words like 'free', 'click', or 'buy now'." ;
            sh:prefixes ( [ sh:namespace "http://schema.org/" ;
                        sh:prefix "schema" ] ) ;
            sh:select """
            SELECT $this
            WHERE {
                $this schema:reviewBody ?body .
                FILTER (regex(?body, "free|click|buy now", "i"))
            }
        """ ] ;
    sh:targetClass schema1:Review .


The SHACL shape :ReviewSpamFilterShape targets all instances of the class schema1:Review and enforces a constraint that each instance must have a schema1:reviewBody property with a value that does not contain any of the spam words 'free', 'click', or 'buy now' (case-insensitive); if this constraint is violated, the validation will produce the message: "Review must not contain spam words like 'free', 'click', or 'buy now'."

:ReviewIntegrityCheckShape a sh:NodeShape ;
    sh:sparql [ a sh:SPARQLConstraint ;
            sh:message "A review cannot contain more than 3 URLs." ;
            sh:prefixes ( [ sh:namespace "http://schema.org/" ;
                        sh:prefix "schema" ] ) ;
            sh:select """
            SELECT $this
            WHERE {
                $this schema:reviewBody ?text .
                BIND((STRLEN(?text) - STRLEN(REPLACE(?text, "http", ""))) AS ?urlCount)
                FILTER(?urlCount > 3)
            }
        """ ] ;
    sh:targetClass schema1:Review .


The SHACL shape :ReviewIntegrityCheckShape applies to all instances of the class schema1:Review, ensuring that the schema:reviewBody property of each review contains no more than 3 URLs, with validation failure resulting in the error message "A review cannot contain more than 3 URLs."

:GrantStatusShape a sh:NodeShape ;
    sh:property [ sh:in ( "Active" "Completed" "Suspended" ) ;
            sh:message "Grant status must be one of: Active, Completed, or Suspended." ;
            sh:path frapo:hasProjectStatus ] ;
    sh:targetClass frapo:ResearchGrant .


The SHACL shape :GrantStatusShape applies to all instances of the class frapo:ResearchGrant, specifying that the property frapo:hasProjectStatus must have exactly one value, which must be one of the following allowed strings: "Active", "Completed", or "Suspended"; if the value does not match one of these allowed statuses, validation will fail with the message: "Grant status must be one of: Active, Completed, or Suspended."

            }
        """ ] ;
    sh:targetClass schema1:MedicalDevice .

    sh:sparql [ a sh:SPARQLConstraint ;
            sh:message "Creator and updater cannot be the same entity." ;
            sh:select """
            SELECT $this WHERE {
                $this dc:creator ?c .
                $this dc:contributor ?u .
                FILTER (?c = ?u)
            }
        """ ] ;
    sh:targetClass dc1:ProvenanceStatement .

Translation #710
@prefix : <http://mapping.example.com/> .
@prefix dc1: <http://purl.org/dc/elements/1.1#> .
@prefix sh: <http://www.w3.org/ns/shacl#> .

:UniqueVersionPerSourceShape a sh:NodeShape ;
    sh:sparql [ a sh:SPARQLConstraint ;
            sh:message "Each source must have unique versions." ;
            sh:select """
            SELECT $this WHERE {
                ?other dc:source ?source ;
                       dc:hasVersion ?version .
                FILTER (?other != $this)
                FILTER EXISTS {
                    $this dc:source ?source ;
                          dc:hasVersion ?version .
                }
            }
        """ ] ;
    sh:targetClass dc1:ProvenanceStatement .


The SHACL shape :UniqueVersionPerSourceShape targets all instances of the class dc1:ProvenanceStatement, enforcing a constraint that ensures each source has unique versions, verified by a SPARQL query which checks that no other provenance statement with the same source and version exists, and producing the message "Each source must have unique versions." if this constraint is violated.

            sh:message "License scope must be consistent with license type." ;

                $this schema:licenseType ?type .

Translation #830
@prefix : <http://mapping.example.com/> .
@prefix schema1: <http://schema.org/> .
@prefix sh: <http://www.w3.org/ns/shacl#> .

:AlertPriorityConsistentWithSeverityShape a sh:NodeShape ;
    sh:sparql [ a sh:SPARQLConstraint ;
            sh:message "Priority must be consistent with severity." ;
            sh:select """
            SELECT $this WHERE {
                $this schema:severity ?severity ;
                      schema:priority ?priority .
                FILTER (
                    (?severity = "Critical" && ?priority != "P1") ||
                    (?severity = "High" && ?priority NOT IN ("P1", "P2")) ||
                    (?severity = "Medium" && ?priority NOT IN ("P3", "P4")) ||
                    (?severity = "Low" && ?priority NOT IN ("P4", "P5"))
                )
            }
        """ ] ;
    sh:targetClass schema1:Event .


The SHACL shape :AlertPriorityConsistentWithSeverityShape applies to all instances of the class schema:Event, enforcing a constraint that ensures the property schema:priority is consistent with the property schema:severity, with specific mappings of severity "Critical" to priority "P1", "High" to priorities "P1" or "P2", "Medium" to priorities "P3" or "P4", and "Low" to priorities "P4" or "P5", and returning the validation error message "Priority must be consistent with severity" if these rules are not met.
----

Translation #832
@prefix : <http://mapping.example.com/> .
@prefix schema1: <http://schema.org/> .
@prefix sh: <http://www.w3.org/ns/shacl#> .

:UniqueAlertIDShape a sh:NodeShape ;
    sh:sparql [ a sh:SPARQLConstraint ;
            sh:message "Alert ID must be unique." ;
            sh:select """
            SELECT $this WHERE {
                ?other a schema:Event ;
                       schema:identifier ?id .
                FILTER (?other != $this)
                FILTER EXISTS {
                    $this schema:identifier ?id .
                }
            }
        """ ] ;
    sh:targetClass schema1:Event .


The SHACL shape :UniqueAlertIDShape targets all instances of the class schema:Event, enforcing a uniqueness constraint on the property schema:identifier, ensuring that each alert ID is unique across all events, and returns an error message "Alert ID must be unique" if a duplicate identifier is found.
----

:AcknowledgedDateAfterAlertDateShape a sh:NodeShape ;
    sh:sparql [ a sh:SPARQLConstraint ;
            sh:message "Acknowledged date must be after alert creation date." ;
            sh:select """
            SELECT $this WHERE {
                $this schema:dateCreated ?created .
                $this schema:dateAcknowledged ?acknowledged .
                FILTER (?acknowledged < ?created)
            }
        """ ] ;
    sh:targetClass schema1:Event .


The SHACL shape :AcknowledgedDateAfterAlertDateShape applies to all instances of the class schema1:Event, specifying a validation rule that checks if the acknowledged date is after the alert creation date, defined by a SPARQL constraint comparing the values of schema:dateAcknowledged and schema:dateCreated properties, with a requirement of exactly one value for each property, failing validation with the message "Acknowledged date must be after alert creation date" if the condition is not met.

:AlertPriorityConsistentWithEscalationShape a sh:NodeShape ;
    sh:sparql [ a sh:SPARQLConstraint ;
            sh:message "Priority must be consistent with escalation level." ;
            sh:select """
            SELECT $this WHERE {
                $this schema:priority ?priority ;
                      schema:escalationLevel ?escalation .
                FILTER (
                    (?priority = "P1" && ?escalation < 4) ||
                    (?priority = "P2" && ?escalation < 3) ||
                    (?priority = "P3" && ?escalation < 2)
                )
            }
        """ ] ;
    sh:targetClass schema1:Event .


Here is the rewritten translation:

The SHACL shape :AlertPriorityConsistentWithEscalationShape targets all instances of the class schema1:Event, enforcing a constraint that requires the value of the property schema:priority to be consistent with the value of the property schema:escalationLevel, specifically: "P1" priority allows escalation levels less than 4, "P2" priority allows escalation levels less than 3, and "P3" priority allows escalation levels less than 2, with validation failure resulting in the message "Priority must be consistent with escalation level."

:AlertSuppressionDateValidShape a sh:NodeShape ;
    sh:sparql [ a sh:SPARQLConstraint ;
            sh:message "Suppression date must be after alert creation date." ;
            sh:select """
            SELECT $this WHERE {
                $this schema:dateCreated ?created .
                $this schema:suppressionUntil ?suppression .
                FILTER (?suppression < ?created)
            }
        """ ] ;
    sh:targetClass schema1:Event .


The SHACL shape :AlertSuppressionDateValidShape targets all instances of the class schema1:Event, enforcing a constraint that each instance must have values for both schema:dateCreated and schema:suppressionUntil, with the latter being strictly after the former; if this temporal relationship is not met, the validation will fail with the message: "Suppression date must be after alert creation date."

Translation #841
@prefix : <http://mapping.example.com/> .
@prefix schema1: <http://schema.org/> .
@prefix sh: <http://www.w3.org/ns/shacl#> .

:AlertPriorityMustMatchSeverityShape a sh:NodeShape ;
    sh:sparql [ a sh:SPARQLConstraint ;
            sh:message "Alert priority must correspond to severity level." ;
            sh:select """
            SELECT $this WHERE {
                $this schema:priority ?priority ;
                      schema:severity ?severity .
                FILTER (
                    (?severity = "Critical" && ?priority != "P1") ||
                    (?severity = "High" && ?priority NOT IN ("P1", "P2")) ||
                    (?severity = "Medium" && ?priority NOT IN ("P3", "P4")) ||
                    (?severity = "Low" && ?priority NOT IN ("P4", "P5"))
                )
            }
        """ ] ;
    sh:targetClass schema1:Event .


The SHACL shape :AlertPriorityMustMatchSeverityShape applies to all instances of the class schema1:Event, requiring that the schema:priority property value corresponds to the schema:severity property value as follows: Critical severity to P1 priority, High severity to either P1 or P2 priority, Medium severity to either P3 or P4 priority, and Low severity to either P4 or P5 priority; if this correspondence is not met, validation will fail with the message "Alert priority must correspond to severity level."
----
